    83|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|        idx = np.random.permutation(N)
    84|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|        no_change = True # Does a change at all in this iteration?  This is not currently being used.

    92|         0|            0|            0|  0.00%|                    z += A[i]
